! Title: [Redacted]'s Supplemental Filter

! URL: [Redacted]

! Note: The sole existence of this version of the list, is because a listmaker who wishes to remain anonymous at the time of writing, has been making a huge and almost entirely unsorted list of his own, complete with some pretty strange choices for sites to block in an allround list. In particular, I wanted to clue him in on that it would maaaaaaaaaaybe be a good idea to move his non-NSFW anti-LBGTQ+ entries (which I of course do not condone) to a separate list. Thus I've done some categorisation for him now.
